\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
detail namespace with internal helper functions 

This namespace collects functions that should not be exposed, implementations of some \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}} methods, and meta-\/programming helpers.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}\label{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}} 
\index{detail@{detail}!value\_t@{value\_t}}
\index{value\_t@{value\_t}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{value\_t}{value\_t}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}{detail\+::value\+\_\+t}} \+: std\+::uint8\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



the JSON type enumeration 

This enumeration collects the different JSON types. It is internally used to distinguish the stored values, and the functions \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ad8789d0a365d5afaab61e7492908d8b2}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+null()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_af355a2b131068acf3d623eb6d80a711c}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+object()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a184ba4a6b47e6da3703af19349bd776f}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+array()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a007ecebde9a7d40714e300ce0ff52908}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+string()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_acfe2e3c359b545f8edbb72f6bd78718c}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+boolean()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aacf244be5088fb183f4ba21a66af9631}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number()}} (with \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a2330e35cda16540058fef090abc709bf}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number\+\_\+integer()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a4de72635745144ee519157d23fe7189a}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number\+\_\+unsigned()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a8d5bb82dfc8cceae1753b52a588eef92}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number\+\_\+float()}}), \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a39e4946a414cc978b88939ed1b343d46}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+discarded()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ad650dd5a7e019b970abce3d8864b5654}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+primitive()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a2d3a5f8761bc6f163f4119bddaf7b092}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+structured()}} rely on it.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
There are three enumeration entries (number\+\_\+integer, number\+\_\+unsigned, and number\+\_\+float), because the library distinguishes these three types for numbers\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ae8505b599e706768a1e0bd6718cc7117}{basic\+\_\+json\+::number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}} is used for unsigned integers, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aba48b0bdee31228a4e19b7c040b6d2a5}{basic\+\_\+json\+::number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}} is used for signed integers, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a80a229dbc84c1334171ce9c49c873c56}{basic\+\_\+json\+::number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}} is used for floating-\/point numbers or to approximate integers which do not fit in the limits of their respective type.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ae2d5bc42270881ed3e219e8b1456fec5}{basic\+\_\+json\+::basic\+\_\+json(const value\+\_\+t value\+\_\+type)}} -- create a JSON \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a47b1bb0bbd3596589ed9187059c312efa2063c1608d6e0baf80249c42e2be5804}{value}} with the default \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a47b1bb0bbd3596589ed9187059c312efa2063c1608d6e0baf80249c42e2be5804}{value}} for a given type
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}\label{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}} 
\index{detail@{detail}!value\_t@{value\_t}}
\index{value\_t@{value\_t}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{value\_t}{value\_t}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}{detail\+::value\+\_\+t}} \+: std\+::uint8\+\_\+t\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



the JSON type enumeration 

This enumeration collects the different JSON types. It is internally used to distinguish the stored values, and the functions \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ad8789d0a365d5afaab61e7492908d8b2}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+null()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_af355a2b131068acf3d623eb6d80a711c}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+object()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a184ba4a6b47e6da3703af19349bd776f}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+array()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a007ecebde9a7d40714e300ce0ff52908}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+string()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_acfe2e3c359b545f8edbb72f6bd78718c}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+boolean()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aacf244be5088fb183f4ba21a66af9631}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number()}} (with \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a2330e35cda16540058fef090abc709bf}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number\+\_\+integer()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a4de72635745144ee519157d23fe7189a}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number\+\_\+unsigned()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a8d5bb82dfc8cceae1753b52a588eef92}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+number\+\_\+float()}}), \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a39e4946a414cc978b88939ed1b343d46}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+discarded()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ad650dd5a7e019b970abce3d8864b5654}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+primitive()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a2d3a5f8761bc6f163f4119bddaf7b092}{basic\+\_\+json\+::is\+\_\+structured()}} rely on it.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
There are three enumeration entries (number\+\_\+integer, number\+\_\+unsigned, and number\+\_\+float), because the library distinguishes these three types for numbers\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ae8505b599e706768a1e0bd6718cc7117}{basic\+\_\+json\+::number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}} is used for unsigned integers, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aba48b0bdee31228a4e19b7c040b6d2a5}{basic\+\_\+json\+::number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}} is used for signed integers, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a80a229dbc84c1334171ce9c49c873c56}{basic\+\_\+json\+::number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}} is used for floating-\/point numbers or to approximate integers which do not fit in the limits of their respective type.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ae2d5bc42270881ed3e219e8b1456fec5}{basic\+\_\+json\+::basic\+\_\+json(const value\+\_\+t value\+\_\+type)}} -- create a JSON \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a47b1bb0bbd3596589ed9187059c312efa2063c1608d6e0baf80249c42e2be5804}{value}} with the default \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a47b1bb0bbd3596589ed9187059c312efa2063c1608d6e0baf80249c42e2be5804}{value}} for a given type
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T , typename U , \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a66bbcd629c83a87ba9cbc72a675cf84a}{enable\+\_\+if\+\_\+t}}$<$ !std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ T, U $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a47b1bb0bbd3596589ed9187059c312efa2063c1608d6e0baf80249c42e2be5804}{\+::value}}, int $>$  = 0$>$ \\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_af2a9ce4740e0b45d33129e2c8e53a0a8}\label{namespacedetail_af2a9ce4740e0b45d33129e2c8e53a0a8}} 
\index{detail@{detail}!escape@{escape}}
\index{escape@{escape}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{escape()}{escape()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename String\+Type $>$ \\
String\+Type detail\+::escape (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String\+Type}]{s }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



string escaping as described in RFC 6901 (Sect. 4) 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em s} & string to escape \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
escaped string
\end{DoxyReturn}
Note the order of escaping \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{} to \char`\"{}$\sim$0\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}/\char`\"{} to \char`\"{}$\sim$1\char`\"{} is important. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_a99cf03d4deaeea599f921f5d23baf0cb}\label{namespacedetail_a99cf03d4deaeea599f921f5d23baf0cb}}

\index{detail@{detail}!hash@{hash}}
\index{hash@{hash}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hash()}{hash()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Basic\+Json\+Type $>$ \\
std\+::size\+\_\+t detail\+::hash (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const Basic\+Json\+Type \&}]{j }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



hash a JSON value 

The hash function tries to rely on std\+::hash where possible. Furthermore, the type of the JSON value is taken into account to have different hash values for null, 0, 0U, and false, etc.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Basic\+Json\+Type} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}} specialization \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em j} & JSON value to hash \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
hash value of j 
\end{DoxyReturn}

constexpr std\+::array$<$ T, sizeof...(Args)$>$ detail\+::make\+\_\+array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Args \&\&...}]{args }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [constexpr]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_aac7ca91589afb0bad68baec5949daaa2}\label{namespacedetail_aac7ca91589afb0bad68baec5949daaa2}} 
\index{detail@{detail}!operator$<$@{operator$<$}}
\index{operator$<$@{operator$<$}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator$<$()}{operator<()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool detail\+::operator$<$ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}{value\+\_\+t}}}]{lhs,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a917c3efabea8a20dc72d9ae2c673d632}{value\+\_\+t}}}]{rhs }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



comparison operator for JSON types 

Returns an ordering that is similar to Python\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item order\+: null \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} boolean \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} number \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} object \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} array \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} string \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} binary
\item furthermore, each type is not smaller than itself
\item discarded values are not comparable
\item binary is represented as a b\char`\"{}\char`\"{} string in python and directly comparable to a string; however, making a binary array directly comparable with a string would be surprising behavior in a JSON file.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_a6fd295e53b1dd4f46e235e6afee26d5e}\label{namespacedetail_a6fd295e53b1dd4f46e235e6afee26d5e}} 
\index{detail@{detail}!replace\_substring@{replace\_substring}}
\index{replace\_substring@{replace\_substring}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{replace\_substring()}{replace\_substring()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename String\+Type $>$ \\
void detail\+::replace\+\_\+substring (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{String\+Type \&}]{s,  }\item[{const String\+Type \&}]{f,  }\item[{const String\+Type \&}]{t }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



replace all occurrences of a substring by another string 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em s} & the string to manipulate; changed so that all occurrences of {\itshape f} are replaced with {\itshape t} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em f} & the substring to replace with {\itshape t} \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em t} & the string to replace {\itshape f} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyPrecond}{Precondition}
The search string {\itshape f} must not be empty. {\bfseries{This precondition is enforced with an assertion.}}
\end{DoxyPrecond}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacedetail_a3f0588f1a546b169113e6e1e293168f4}\label{namespacedetail_a3f0588f1a546b169113e6e1e293168f4}} 
\index{detail@{detail}!to\_chars@{to\_chars}}
\index{to\_chars@{to\_chars}!detail@{detail}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_chars()}{to\_chars()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Float\+Type $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{pi_offboard_stereo_vision_2src_2json_8hpp_a5f2aaec3b681d0a72f7d6e90b70cdcd1}{JSON\+\_\+\+HEDLEY\+\_\+\+RETURNS\+\_\+\+NON\+\_\+\+NULL}} char $\ast$ detail\+::to\+\_\+chars (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{char $\ast$}]{first,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{last,  }\item[{Float\+Type}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



generates a decimal representation of the floating-\/point number value in \mbox{[}first, last). 

The format of the resulting decimal representation is similar to printf\textquotesingle{}s g format. Returns an iterator pointing past-\/the-\/end of the decimal representation.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The input number must be finite, i.\+e. NaN\textquotesingle{}s and Inf\textquotesingle{}s are not supported. 

The buffer must be large enough. 

The result is NOT null-\/terminated. 
\end{DoxyNote}
